This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)


This is previous problem file:

    (door-open pantry kitchen east)

    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)

 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )

      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)


This is previous problem file: 
(define (problem explore-kitchen-corridor)
  (:domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:objects kitchen pantry - location
            east west north south - direction)
  (:init
    (at kitchen)
    (explored kitchen)
    (explored pantry)
    (door-between kitchen pantry west)
    (door-between pantry kitchen east)
    (door-open kitchen pantry west)
    (door-open pantry kitchen east)
  )
  (:goal (at pantry))
)

 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )

 (define (problem explore-kitchen-corridor)
  (:domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:objects kitchen pantry corridor living-room - location
            east west north south - direction)
  (:init
    (at pantry)
    (explored kitchen)
    (explored pantry)
    (door-between kitchen pantry west)
    (door-between pantry kitchen east)
    (door-open kitchen pantry west)
    (door-open pantry kitchen east)
    (door-between kitchen corridor north)
    (door-closed kitchen corridor north)
    (door-between kitchen living-room south)
    (door-closed kitchen living-room south)
  )
  (:goal (at corridor))
)

 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)


This is previous problem file: 
(define (problem explore-kitchen-corridor)
  (:domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:objects kitchen pantry living-room - location
            east west north south - direction)
  (:init
    (at pantry)
    (explored kitchen)
    (explored pantry)
    (door-between kitchen pantry west)
    (door-between pantry kitchen east)
    (door-open kitchen pantry west)
    (door-open pantry kitchen east)
    (door-between kitchen living-room south)
  )
  (:goal (at living-room))
)

  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)

  )

      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)

(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

           east west north south - direction)

    (at backyard)
    (explored backyard)
    (explored corridor)
    (explored kitchen)
    (explored pantry)
    ;; kitchen and pantry connection (open frosted-glass door)
    (door-between kitchen pantry west)
    (door-between pantry kitchen east)
    (door-open kitchen pantry west)
    (door-open pantry kitchen east)

    (door-between kitchen living-room south)
    (door-between living-room kitchen north)

    (door-between kitchen corridor north)
    (door-between corridor kitchen south)
    (door-open kitchen corridor north)
    (door-open corridor kitchen south)
    ;; corridor <-> backyard connection (north, open sliding patio door)
    (door-between corridor backyard north)
    (door-between backyard corridor south)
    (door-open corridor backyard north)
    (door-open backyard corridor south)
    ;; backyard north to driveway (assume always open, since described as visible)
    (door-between backyard driveway north)
    (door-between driveway backyard south)
    (door-open backyard driveway north)
    (door-open driveway backyard south)
    ;; backyard east to street (assume always open, since described as visible)

    (door-between street backyard west)
    (door-open backyard street east)
    (door-open street backyard west)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

(define (problem explore-backyard-unvisited)
  (:domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:objects kitchen pantry living-room corridor backyard driveway street unknown-east-door-loc unknown-west-door-loc - location
           east west north south - direction)
  (:init
    (at backyard)
    (explored backyard)
    (explored corridor)
    (explored kitchen)
    (explored pantry)
    ;; kitchen and pantry connection (open frosted-glass door)
    (door-between kitchen pantry west)
    (door-between pantry kitchen east)
    (door-open kitchen pantry west)
    (door-open pantry kitchen east)
    ;; kitchen and living-room connection (south, always open)
    (door-between kitchen living-room south)
    (door-between living-room kitchen north)
    (door-open kitchen living-room south)
    (door-open living-room kitchen north)
    ;; kitchen and corridor connection (north, open)
    (door-between kitchen corridor north)
    (door-between corridor kitchen south)
    (door-open kitchen corridor north)
    (door-open corridor kitchen south)
    ;; corridor <-> backyard connection (north, open sliding patio door)
    (door-between corridor backyard north)
    (door-between backyard corridor south)
    (door-open corridor backyard north)
    (door-open backyard corridor south)
    ;; backyard north to driveway (assume always open, since described as visible)
    (door-between backyard driveway north)
    (door-between driveway backyard south)
    (door-open backyard driveway north)
    (door-open driveway backyard south)
    ;; backyard east to street (assume always open, since described as visible)
    (door-between backyard street east)

(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

(define (problem explore-unvisited-north-of-street)
  (:domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:objects kitchen pantry living-room corridor backyard driveway street unknown-east-door-loc unknown-west-door-loc unknown-north-street-door-loc - location
           east west north south - direction)
  (:init
    (at street)
    (explored street)
    (explored driveway)
    (explored backyard)
    (explored corridor)
    (explored kitchen)
    (explored pantry)
    ;; kitchen and pantry connection (open frosted-glass door)
    (door-between kitchen pantry west)
    (door-between pantry kitchen east)
    (door-open kitchen pantry west)
    (door-open pantry kitchen east)
    ;; kitchen and living-room connection (south, always open)
    (door-between kitchen living-room south)
    (door-between living-room kitchen north)
    (door-open kitchen living-room south)
    (door-open living-room kitchen north)
    ;; kitchen and corridor connection (north, open)
    (door-between kitchen corridor north)
    (door-between corridor kitchen south)
    (door-open kitchen corridor north)
    (door-open corridor kitchen south)
    ;; corridor <-> backyard connection (north, open sliding patio door)
    (door-between corridor backyard north)
    (door-between backyard corridor south)
    (door-open corridor backyard north)
    (door-open backyard corridor south)
    ;; backyard north to driveway (always open)
    (door-between backyard driveway north)
    (door-between driveway backyard south)
    (door-open backyard driveway north)
    (door-open driveway backyard south)
    ;; backyard east to street (always open, visible from backyard)
    (door-between backyard street east)
    (door-between street backyard west)
    (door-open backyard street east)
    (door-open street backyard west)
    ;; corridor east closed wood door
    (door-between corridor unknown-east-door-loc east)
    (door-between unknown-east-door-loc corridor west)
    (door-closed corridor unknown-east-door-loc east)
    (door-closed unknown-east-door-loc corridor west)
    ;; corridor west closed wood door
    (door-between corridor unknown-west-door-loc west)
    (door-between unknown-west-door-loc corridor east)
    (door-closed corridor unknown-west-door-loc west)
    (door-closed unknown-west-door-loc corridor east)

    (door-between unknown-north-street-door-loc street south)
    (door-closed street unknown-north-street-door-loc north)

  )

 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain partial-observable-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door-between ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (explored ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
      :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door-between ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir))
      :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )

  (:action move
      :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
      :precondition (and (at ?from) (door-between ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
      :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (explored ?to))
  )
)
